### Database/migrations

Parent schema is the B-1 SQLite migration `20260718050000_vision_waypoint_b1` / MySQL `0005_vision_waypoint_b1`.

B2 adds:

- SQLite `20260718090000_vision_capture_b2`
- MySQL `0006_vision_capture_b2`

Changes:

- `VisionCaptureSession`: unique nullable `sessionKey`, protocol/capture API, target/quality/interruption JSON metadata, manifest version, updated timestamp.
- `VisionRecordingAsset`: media type, manifest version/body, duration.
- New `VisionCaptureInterruption` with cascade FK.
- New `VisionDiagnosticBundle` with nullable `SET NULL` FK.
- New `VisionCapturePreference` with unique owner/device key.

The migration is additive and correctly ordered after B-1. Creator-manifest persistence is transactional, checks owned draft state, writes session/asset/interruption/audit records, and tombstones deletion.

Integration concerns:

- `VisionCapturePreference` is schema-only; hotkey, preview, and retention controls do not use it.
- `VisionDiagnosticBundle` is schema-only; native diagnostics remain local gzip metadata.
- B-1 Prisma `CompanionDevice`/`PairingSession` are not used by B2; pairing metadata instead persists in app-data JSON.
- Live MySQL execution was not demonstrated.
- Preserve B-1 → B2 order; reconcile later independent migrations rather than timestamp-sorting.

### Contracts and architecture

Implemented contracts/symbols include:

- Capture protocol `2.0`, core `0.4.0-b2`.
- States from `IDLE` through `TARGET_LOST`.
- Capture-only results:
  - `EVIDENCE_CAPTURED`
  - `INSUFFICIENT_CAPTURE_EVIDENCE`
  - `CAPTURE_CANCELLED`
  - `CAPTURE_ERROR`
- `CapturePlatformAdapter`, `DesktopCapturePlatformAdapter`, `WebCapturePlatformAdapter`.
- Strict capability/status/target/envelope Zod schemas.
- Narrow desktop and browser command allowlists.
- Exact-origin ECDSA P-256 challenge pairing with expiry, replay protection, revocation, rate and payload limits.
- Bounded 84-frame/32 MiB player ring, 3–8 second scan, 8–12 FPS, 3–12 selected metadata frames.
- Creator WebM + strict manifest + SHA-256 under Electron user data.
- Metadata-only diagnostic export.
- Real selected-window capture through Electron `desktopCapturer`; capability honestly reports `ELECTRON_DESKTOP_CAPTURER`, not a guaranteed lower-level WGC implementation.

Material consolidation issues:

1. B2 has two capture-contract implementations: Zod/TypeScript in `src/vision/capture-protocol.ts` and a handwritten CJS validator in `apps/companion/capture-contract.cjs`. Constants, states, commands, payload rules, and errors are duplicated with no parity test or generation path.
2. B1 protocol `1.0` and B2 capture protocol `2.0` are intentionally versioned separately, but their compatibility/ownership must be documented in the canonical protocol package.
3. B2 creates a parallel `CapturePlatformAdapter` instead of composing capture into the authoritative B-1 `VisionPlatformAdapter`.
4. `src/vision/platform-adapters.ts` broadens desktop `invoke` from a typed union to arbitrary `string`; retain runtime allowlisting but do not preserve this type weakening.
5. B2 flag names are phase-local snake-case/env flags, not the requested final canonical dotted flag namespace.

### Source-supported gaps and risks

- Feature flags are not enforced by the native core:
  - packaged desktop startup overwrites seven `FEATURE_*` values to `"1"`;
  - coordinator commands do not check them;
  - the dashboard does not condition controls on individual capture flags.
  - Therefore documented rollback-by-setting-flags-to-0 is false for the packaged shell.
- Capture health lacks an active timer/heartbeat. `frameAgeMs` is computed only when status/progress is requested, while progress is frame-driven. A stalled stream can stop emitting updates until auto-finalization, so “ongoing truthful frozen health” is only partially implemented.
- The roadmap-required mock result continuing through the B-1 story path is not demonstrated. B2 returns capture-only metadata and modifies the B-1 endpoint gate, but no capture result is passed through canonical B-1 progression.
- Global hotkey is configurable only among three presets; physical hold/release in-game remains untested.
- Preferences and diagnostic database entities have no production service consumers.
- The standalone dashboard has its own Harbor/Studio/Player navigation and phase-specific CSS. Port behavior into the current canonical shell/design system rather than restoring it wholesale.
- Player UI is a test harness, not canonical journal/story integration; that later runtime binding is explicitly deferred.
- `companion:test`, native Electron smoke, and hotkey smoke are not invoked by `scripts/test-all.ps1`; their evidence was run separately and must be retained as explicit validation gates.

### Test claims versus reproducible source evidence

The report claims:

- 35 Vitest files / 106 tests;
- 20 Companion Node tests;
- 3 desktop tests;
- 7 SQLite migrations and persistence proof;
- 26 Playwright passes / 8 intentional WebKit skips;
- real selected-window capture, browser-paired scan, hotkey registration/conflict;
- desktop build;
- final packaged execution blocked.

Static source confirms the tests and harnesses exist. The one Playwright B2 test only verifies the unpaired browser surface and privacy text; actual pairing/capture is exercised by the Node loopback test and Electron smoke, not Playwright.

No tests were rerun in this lane. Claimed prior evidence is therefore historical, not current reproduced evidence.

Original exit gate has 62 rows. The completion report marks 58 PASS and four BLOCKED:

1. real Sea of Thieves selection;
2. physical monitor movement/DPI/resizing ceremony;
3. representative gameplay performance;
4. physical hotkey release.

That gives a documented maximum of `58/62 = 93.5%`, not completion. Accounting for the flag enforcement, duplicate-contract, heartbeat, and missing B-1 story-path proof, my source-backed assessment is approximately **85% implemented**, with **production readiness: no**.

### Current-main overlap and stale-base risk

Current committed `main` is `fb8eb4ac33f4a44028fe82fb08df0ac0e5021db6`.

- B2 changed 73 paths from B-1.
- Committed `main` changed 45 paths since the merge base.
- Only three committed overlaps exist, all chat-sync state:
  - B-1 transcript
  - `Codex_Chats/manifest.json`
  - latest sync report.
- Current canonical uncommitted work overlaps three B2 source/config paths:
  - `eslint.config.mjs`
  - `scripts/test-all.ps1`
  - `src/app/layout.tsx`

Thus most capture code is additive, but shared configuration, schema, package/lock, feature flags, platform adapters, root layout, service worker, CSP, and newer canonical shell work require semantic integration.

### Include/exclude/extract recommendation

Include:

- native Companion core, storage, target worker, loopback pairing, hotkey/HWND monitor;
- capture-only protocol behavior and tests;
- desktop IPC/coordinator integration;
- persistence APIs/service and both migrations;
- PWA cache protection and CSP intent;
- all B2 ADRs and engineering records.

Adapt before acceptance:

- unify TS/CJS capture contracts;
- compose capture into the canonical platform interface;
- restore typed IPC command contracts;
- make flags authoritative and actually stop/deny native operations;
- add a real health heartbeat;
- port dashboard functions into the current shell/design system;
- wire or explicitly defer the B-1 mock-story demonstration;
- decide whether preferences, pairing, and diagnostic metadata belong in Prisma or local app data;
- regenerate the lockfile once under the package owner.

Exclude from direct cherry-pick:

- the three chat-sync state paths in `eec2c73`;
- ignored builds, caches, `.env`, databases, installers, screenshots, and validation output.

Confidence: high on provenance, commit classification, source inventory, and identified gaps; medium-high on completion percentage because no test suite or native runtime was authorized in this lane.
